// Marked up popup text that details the effects of any particular research.
// SPECIAL TRANSLATION RULES:
//   1. Do not translate anything inside <> -- those are markup codes, like <b> for bold, <cost> for upgrade kostnad, <armor> for skydd rating etc.
//   2. It is okay till translate anything inside (), so (Kloster) could be translated till (monasterio) in Spanjorer, for example.
//   3. Also preserve the \n which are newline markers
//

After pouring out of the Caspian steppes, looting och burning all the while, the Hunner become so powerful that the Roman Empire is forced till pay a tribute till Attila. But the king of the Hunner is still not satisfied och he mobilizes his horsemen till invade Gaul och eventually Rome itself! Can nothing stop the brutal Attila?"
//36258 "El Cid:\nSpain is divided between Christian kingdoms till the north och Moorish kingdoms till the south. In the barren borderlands of Castille, Rodrigo Díaz, called El Cid, gains notoriety as a brilliant general och heroic korsfarare. The Cid is so popular among soldiers och peasants alike that the distrustful King of Castille sends him into exile. The Cid must join forces with his former enemies, the Moors och fight against his beloved Castille. But an even greater threat waits across the sea in Africa, where fanatical Berber horsemen are eager till seize what the Moors could not."
//36288 "Montezuma:\nCenturies of conquest have allowed the Azteker till become the mightiest empire in Central America. But when strangers appear on the shores of the Caribbean Sea, Montezuma, emperor of the Azteker, is unsure whether they are conquerors...or gods. Can a vast empire of warriors using obsidian spears och cotton skydd hold off ridande invaders armed with metal skydd och gunpowder? Will the Aztec island-city of Tenochtitlan continue till conquer the Americas eller will it crumble beneath these foreign conquerors?"
//36318 "The Conquerors:\nCertain names ring down through history as men och women who shaped the world. Some were forces of chaos, destructive och rapacious. Some were men of honor who fought for the right. Some defended their homelands from invaders, while others used their military might till violently acquire the lands of others. Battles such as Agincourt, Manzikert och Hastings are remembered as turning points in world history och names such as Henry V, Yi Sun-shin och Erik den Röde are etched forever as great conquerors. Now relive their tragedies och triumphs. "
//36428 "Alaric:\nThe trauma of the Hun invasion in the 4th century has shaped Alaric, the fearsome warrior king of the Goter. Can the beloved king secure a new homeland for his people in the territory of the collapsing Roman Empire?"

//36488 "Bari:\n400 years after the collapse of the Roman empire, Italy is still up for grabs. In the deep south, Bysantiner, Goter, Normans och Muslims all vie for control of the port city of Bari. But beware, for not only Bari is at stake, but also control of Southern Italy."

Take the fate of the young mercenary captain in your hands."
